  \n  \n    Do not post: \n    \nContent about non-medical drugs that\n  \n   \n      Coordinates or encourages others to sell non-medical drugs \n      Depicts, admits to, attempts purchase, or promotes sales of non-medical drugs by the poster of the content or their associates \n     Promotes, encourages, coordinates, or provides instructions for use or make of non-medical drugs \n      Admits, either in writing or verbally, to personal use of non-medical drugs unless posted in a recovery context \n  \n  \n     \n Content that depicts the sale or attempt to purchase marijuana and pharmaceutical drugs. This includes content that\n    \n       Mentions or depicts marijuana or pharmaceutical drugs \n       Makes an attempt to sell or trade, by which we mean any of the following:\n         \n           Explicitly mentioning the product is for sale or trade or delivery \n           Asking the audience to buy \n           Listing the price \n           Encouraging contact about the product either by explicitly asking to be contacted or including any type of contact information \n           Attempting to solicit the product, defined as:\n             \n               Stating interest in buying the product, or \n               Asking if anyone has the product for sale\/trade \n             \n            \n         \n       \n       This applies to both individual pieces of content and Pages and Groups primarily dedicated to the sale of marijuana or pharmaceutical drugs \n     \n\n      Content that attempts to offer, sell, gift, exchange, or transfer firearms, firearm parts, ammunition, or explosives between private individuals, unless posted by a Page representing a real brick-and-mortar store, legitimate website, brand or government agency (e.g. police department, fire department). This includes content that:\n   \n     Mentions or depicts firearms, firearm parts, ammunition, explosives, or 3D gun printing files of any firearm or its parts * , and \n     Makes an attempt to sell or trade, by which we mean:\n       \n         Explicitly mentioning the product is for sale or trade, or \n         Asking the audience to buy, or \n         Listing the price or noting that the product is free \n         Encouraging contact about the product either by\n           \n             Explicitly asking to be contacted \n             Including any type of contact information \n           \n          \n         Making an attempt to solicit the item for sale, defined as\n           \n             Stating that they are interested in buying the good, or \n             Asking if anyone else has the good for sale\/trade \n           \n                   \n       \n      \n     *  3D gun printing files or instructions to manufacture firearms using 3D printers or CNC milling machines, including links to websites where such files or instructions are made available, may not be shared by anyone.   \n     Every day, people use Facebook to share their experiences, connect with friends and family, and build communities. We are a service for more than two billion people to freely express themselves across countries and cultures and in dozens of languages. \n     We recognize how important it is for Facebook to be a place where people feel empowered to communicate, and we take seriously our role in keeping abuse off our service. That\u2019s why we\u2019ve  developed a set of Community Standards  that outline what is and is not allowed on Facebook. Our policies are based on feedback from our community and the advice of experts in fields such as technology, public safety and human rights. To ensure that everyone\u2019s voice is valued, we take great care to craft policies that are inclusive of different views and beliefs, in particular those of people and communities that might otherwise be overlooked or marginalized. \n   \n         \n     VOICE \n     The goal of our Community Standards is to  create a place for expression and give people a voice . Building community and bringing the world closer together depends on people\u2019s ability to share diverse views, experiences, ideas and information. We want people to be able to talk openly about the issues that matter to them, even if some may disagree or find them objectionable. In some cases, we allow content which would otherwise go against our Community Standards \u2013 if it is newsworthy and in the public interest. We do this only after weighing the public interest value against the risk of harm and we look to international human rights standards to make these judgments.  \n    \n     Our commitment to expression is paramount, but we recognize the internet creates new and increased opportunities for abuse. For these reasons, when we limit expression, we do it in service of one or more the following values: \n   \n       \n\n     Authenticity:  We want to make sure the content people are seeing on Facebook is authentic. We believe that authenticity creates a better environment for sharing, and that\u2019s why we don\u2019t want people using Facebook to misrepresent who they are or what they\u2019re doing.\n \n    \n    \n      \n    \n     Safety:  We are committed to making Facebook a safe place. Expression that threatens people has the potential to intimidate, exclude or silence others and isn\u2019t allowed on Facebook. \n  \n    \n  \n    \n    \n     Privacy:  We are committed to protecting personal privacy and information. Privacy gives people the freedom to be themselves, and to choose how and when to share on Facebook and to connect more easily.\n \n        \n  \n    \n     Dignity:  We believe that all people are equal in dignity and rights. We expect that people will respect the dignity of others and not harass or degrade others. \n    \n\n\n    \n    \n     Our Community Standards apply to everyone, all around the world, and to all types of content. They\u2019re designed to be comprehensive \u2013 for example, content that might not be considered hateful may still be removed for violating a different policy. We recognize that words mean different things or affect people differently depending on their local community, language, or background. We work hard to account for these nuances while also applying our policies consistently and fairly to people and their expression. \n\n     People can report potentially violating content, including Pages, Groups, Profiles, individual content, and comments. We also give people control over their own experience by allowing them to\n       block ,   unfollow \n       or \n        hide  people and posts.\n       \n\n     The consequences for violating our Community Standards vary depending on the severity of the violation and the person's history on the platform. For instance, we may warn someone for a first violation, but if they continue to violate our policies, we may restrict their ability to post on Facebook or disable their profile. We also may notify law enforcement when we believe there is a genuine risk of physical harm or a direct threat to public safety. \n     Our Community Standards are a guide for what is and isn\u2019t allowed on Facebook. It is in this spirit that we ask members of the Facebook community to follow these guidelines. \n   \n premeditados contra personas o propiedades a fin de intimidar a la poblaci\u00f3n civil, el gobierno u organizaciones internacionales, con un prop\u00f3sito pol\u00edtico, religioso o ideol\u00f3gico acto de violencia premeditada contra personas o propiedades ejecutado por un agente no gubernamental a fin de intimidar a la poblaci\u00f3n civil, el gobierno u organizaciones internacionales, con prop\u00f3sitos pol\u00edticos, religiosos o ideol\u00f3gicos. \n     \n   \n \n \n     \n \nOrganizaciones que incitan al odio y sus l\u00edderes y miembros prominentes     \n \n   Una o manifiesto o haya realizado acciones f\u00edsicas en ataque a personas por caracter\u00edsticas que incluyen raza, religi\u00f3n, nacionalidad, etnia, g\u00e9nero, sexo, orientaci\u00f3n sexual o enfermedad o discapacidad grave. \n     \n     \n \n \n     \n Asesinos en masa o en serie\n\t \n     Consideramos que un homicidio es un asesinato en masa si en un incidente provoca cuatro o m\u00e1s muertes \n     Consideramos asesino en serie a cualquier persona que haya cometido dos o m\u00e1s asesinatos en diferentes incidentes o ubicaciones. \n     Evaluamos todo lo anterior a partir de la informaci\u00f3n que tenemos disponible y, por lo general, aplicaremos esta pol\u00edtica a todo asesino en serie que re\u00fana cualquiera de estos criterios:\n    \t \n     \t    Recibi\u00f3 una sentencia por asesinato en masa o en serie \n          Fue asesinado por las autoridades durante la ejecuci\u00f3n de un asesinato en masa o en serie o durante su posterior huida \n          Se suicid\u00f3 en la escena del asesinato en masa o en serie o en el per\u00edodo posterior a este \n          Fue identificado por las autoridades competentes con im\u00e1genes obtenidas del crimen \n
